Jamison Brereton

91 (917)
Agni
Aruс╣Зa Vaitahavya
15 verses: jagat─л, except triс╣гс╣нubh 15
This hymn is reminiscent of X.89 in style: a well-crafted, self-consciously rhetorical praise of the god utilizing standard tropes and traditional images. The poet of this hymn is especially fond of etymological figures (especially in the first few verses) and chaining between verses (note, e.g., vss. 8d/9a, 10/11).
The hymn covers many familiar themes, contrasting the physical fire (e.g., vss. 5тАУ7) with the deified fire and his ritual roles, but it is the latter aspect of Agni that is dominant.

Wilson

English translation:
10.091.01 Dam┼лnas, being glorified by his diligent (worshippers), desiring food upon the footmark of Iс╕╖─Б, iskindled in the chamber (of sacrifice), the offerer of every oblation, the object of veneration, the lord, theresplendent, to him who desires his friendship.

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Dam┼лnas: an epithet of Agni; genitive rous or submissive

Jamison Brereton

Awakening, he is kindled by the wakeful ones, the household master in the house, becoming refreshed in the footprint of refreshment,
the Hotar of every oblation, worthy to be chosen, far-ranging,
far-radiant, a good comrade to one who acts as comrade.

Griffith

BRISK, at the place of Ila, hymned by men who wake, our own familiar Friend is kindled in the house;
Hotar of all oblation, worthy of our choice, Lord, beaming, trusty friend to one who loveth him.

Geldner

Von den Fr├╝hwachen wird der Erwachende gemeinsam entz├╝ndet im Hause der Hausgebieter an der St├дtte der Id Labung, die Opferspende genie├Яend, der zu erw├дhlende Opferpriester jeglichen Opfers, machtvoll, erstrahlend, ein guter Freund dem, der wie ein guter Freund handelt.

Grassmann

Entz├╝ndet wird von wachenden der rauschende, im Haus der rege Hausfreund an der Andacht Ort Der Opferer jedweden Tranks, der liebliche, der kr├дftig strahlt, ein lieber Freund dem, der ihn liebt.

Elizarenkova

He, with beauty lovely to see, a guest in every houseтАФin every (piece of) wood he is set like (a bird) of swooping pursuit in the woods.
Belonging to the people, he does not overlook any people. Belonging to the clan, he dwells among the clansтАФeach and every clan.

Griffith

He, excellent in glory, guest in every house, finds like a swift-winged bird a home in every tree.
Benevolent to men, he scorns no living man: Friend to the tribes of men he dwells with every tribe.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬYou, Agni, are vigorous with vigour, you are active with acts (of piety), you are wise with wisdom,knowing all things. You are the dispenser of wealth, you abide alone, you are lord of the treasures of heaven andearth.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Very skillful through your skills, through your will you are strong-willed. O Agni, you are the all-knowing poet through your poetic craft.
As good one, you alone hold sway over goods, which both Heaven and Earth foster.

Griffith

Most sage with insight, passing skilful with thy powers art thou, O Agni, wise with wisdom, knowing all.
As Vasu, thou alone art Lord of all good things, of all the treasures that the heavens and earth produce.

Geldner

Grassmann

Durch Kr├дfte bist du kr├дftig und durch Klugheit klug, allweise, Agni, Seher du durch Seherkraft, Du bist allein, o guter, alles Gutes Herr, das auf der Erde, in dem Himmel sch├╢n erbl├╝ht.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬSagacious Agni, you sit at your station suited to the sacrifice and anointed with butter at the foot-markof Iс╕╖─Б. your quick-moving rays are manifested like those of the dawns, beautiful as those of the sun.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Foresightful, o Agni, you have settled down seasonably to your
ghee-rich womb, in the footprint of refreshment.
Your arrivals show brightly like those of the dawns, your reins spotless like the rays of the sun.

Griffith

Foreknowing well, O Agni, thou in Ila’s place hast occupied thy regular station balmed with oil.
Marked are thy comings like the comings of the Dawns, the rays of him who shineth spotless as the Sun.

Geldner

Dich auskennend hast du dich, Agni, in deinen zeitgem├д├Яen Scho├Я, den schmalzigen, an der St├дtte der Ila gesetzt. Deine Ankunft ist pr├дchtig wie die der Usas, makellos wie die Strahlen der Sonne.

Grassmann

Wohl kennend, Agni, deinen regelrechten Sitz, den butterreichen, nahmst du Platz am Andachtsort, Es gl├дnzten deine Bahnen wie des Morgenroths und wie der Sonne fleckenloser Strahlenschein.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬYour glories, Agni, like the lightnings of the rain-cloud are manifested many-tinted, like themanifestations of the dawn, when quitting the plural nts and the forests, you gather on all sides food for your mouth.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Your beauties, brilliant like the lightning flashes of a rain-bearing (cloud), show brightly like the beacons of the dawns,
when, set loose toward the plants and woods, you encompass them
yourself as food in your mouth.

Griffith

Thy glories are, as lightnings from the rainy cloud, marked, many-hued, like heralds of the Dawns’ approach,
When, loosed to wander over plants and forest trees, thou crammest by thyself thy food into thy mouth.

рдЛрддреНрд╡рд┐рдпрдореН рдЛрддреМ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрдВ рдЧрд░реНрднрдВ рдЧрд░реНрднрднреВрддрдВ рддрдВ рдкреНрд░рдХреГрддрдордЧреНрдирд┐рдореН рдУрд╖рдзреАрдГ рдУрд╖рдзреНрдпрдГ рджрдзрд┐рд░реЗ рдзрд╛рд░рдпрдиреНрддрд┐ ред рддрдореН рдПрд╡ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рдВ рдорд╛рддрд░рдГ рдзрд╛рд░рдХрддреНрд╡реЗрди рдорд╛рддреГрд╕реНрдерд╛рдиреАрдпрд╛ рдЖрдкрдГ рдЪ рдЬрдирдпрдиреНрдд рдЬрдирдпрдиреНрддрд┐ ред рдХрд┐рдВрдЪ рд╡рдирд┐рдирдГ рд╡рдирд╕реНрдкрддрдпрдГ рдЪ рд╕рдорд╛рдирдВ рдЧрд░реНрднрднрд╛рд╡реЗрди рдкреНрд░рд╡реЗрд╢рд╛рддреН рд╕реНрд╡рддреБрд▓реНрдпрдВ рддрдорд┐рддреН рддрдореЗрд╡рд╛рдЧреНрдирд┐рдВ рдЬрдирдпрдиреНрддрд┐ ред рдХрд┐рдВрдЪ рддрдореЗрд╡рд╛рдЧреНрдирд┐рдореН рдЕрдиреНрддрд░реНрд╡рддреАрдГ рдЧрд░реНрднрд╡рддреНрдпрдГ рд╡реАрд░реБрдзрдГ рдУрд╖рдзрдпрдГ рдЪ рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╣рд╛ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рджрд╛ рд╕реБрд╡рддреЗ рдЬрдирдпрдиреНрддрд┐ рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThe plural nts bear him as the embryo (conceived) in due season; the maternal waters bring forth Agni;yes, the trees and the pregnant creepers bring him forth daily like themselves.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Sam─Бnam = equal to (or like)themselves, since he enters them as an embryo

Jamison Brereton

The plants conceived him as their embryo at the proper season; the waters as his mothers begot this Agni.
Both the woody (plants) and the sprouts (become) pregnant and give birth to him who is just the same everywhere.

Griffith

Him, duly coming as their germ, have plants received: this Agni have maternal Waters brought to life.
So in like manner do the forest trees and plants bear him within them and produce him evermore.

Geldner

Ihn empfingen die Pflanzen als rechtzeitige Leibesfrucht; den Agni erzeugten die Gew├дsser als seine Mutter. Mit ihm gehen gleichm├д├Яig die B├дume und die Gew├дchse schwanger und geb├дren ihn allezeit.

Grassmann

Als Keim empfingen Pflanzen ihn zu rechter Zeit, als M├╝tter haben die Gew├дsser ihn erzeugt, Denselben nun die B├дume und die Kr├дuter auch, und immerdar geb├дren ihn die schwangeren.

Elizarenkova

рд╕рд╛рдпрдг-рднрд╛рд╖реНрдпрдореН

рд╣реЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдиреЗ рдпрддреН рдпрджрд╛ рддреНрд╡рдВ рд╡рд╛рддреЛрдкрдзреВрддрдГ рд╡рд╛рдпреБрдирд╛ рдХрдореНрдкрд┐рддрдГ рд╡рд╢рд╛рдиреН рдХрд╛рдиреНрддрд╛рдиреН рд╡рдирд╕реНрдкрддреАрдиреН рдЕрдиреБ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐ рддреГрд╖реБ рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдкреНрд░рдореН рдЗрд╖рд┐рддрдГ рдкреНрд░реЗрд░рд┐рддрд╢реНрдЪ рд╕рдиреН рдЕрдиреНрдирд╛ рдЕрджрдиреАрдпрд╛рдирд┐ рд╡рдирд╕реНрдкрддреНрдпрд╛рджреАрдирд┐ рд╕реНрдерд╛рд╡рд░рд╛рдгрд┐ рд╡реЗрд╡рд┐рд╖рддреН рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдкреНрдиреБрд╡рдиреН рд╡рд┐рддрд┐рд╖реНрдард╕реЗ рдЗрддрд╕реНрддрддреЛ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрд╕рд┐ рддрджрд╛рдиреАрдВ рдзрдХреНрд╖рддрдГ рдХрд╛рд╖реНрдард╛рдирд┐ рджрд╣рддрдГ рддреЗ рддрд╡ рдЕрдЬрд░рд╛рдгрд┐ рдЬрд░рд╛рд░рд╣рд┐рддрд╛рдирд┐ рд╢рд░реНрдзрд╛рдВрд╕рд┐ рддреЗрдЬрд╛рдВрд╕рд┐ рдпрдерд╛ рд░рдереНрдпрдГ рд░рдерд┐рдирдГ рддрджреНрд╡рддреН рдкреГрдердХреН рдЖ рдпрддрдиреНрддреЗ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрдиреНрддрд┐ рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬWhen, agitated by the wind and quickly moving through the beloved (trees), you spread aboutdevouring the food, the imperishable energies of you, Agni, the devourer, rush forth like charioteers.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

When whipped up by the wind, aroused, you spread yourself out, constantly worrying the dry food at will,
your unaging troops [=flames] take up their places separately like
charioteers, as you go burning, Agni.

Griffith

When, sped and urged by wind, thou spreadest thee abroad, swift piercing through thy food according to thy will,
Thy never-ceasing blazes, longing to consume, like men on chariots, Agni, strive on every side.

Geldner

Wann du vom Winde angefacht, zur Eile getrieben, nach Belieben gierig die Speisen verarbeitend dich ausbreitest, dann nehmen deine ewig jungen Heerhaufen wie Wagenfahrer getrennt Aufstellung, o Agni, w├дhrend du brennst.

Grassmann

Wenn gierig du vom Wind bewegt nach Wunsch dich regst, und deine Speisen rasch ergreifend weiter dringst, Dann streben deine Flammen Wagenlenkern gleich, die ewig muntern, Agni, vorw├дrts hier und dort.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬ(The priest) selects you, (Agni), the giver of intelligence, the accomplisher of the sacrifice, the invokerof the gods, the chief overcomer of foes, the councillor, alike verily at the lesser and at the greater oblation andnone other than you.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Creator of wisdom, furtherer of the rite, Agni, the Hotar, best
encompassing thought,
just him at the small oblation, just the same for the great oneтАФjust him they chooseтАФno other than you.

Griffith

Agni, the Hotar-priest who fills the assembly full, Waker of knowledge, chief Controller of the thought,-
Him, yea, none other than thyself, doth man elect at sacrificial offerings great and small alike.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThe performers of sacred rites, devoted to Agni, to you, select you as the ministrant priest at sacrificesin this world, when the devout worshippers bearing oblations and strewing the clipped sacred grass offer youfood.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Just you do they choose hereтАФthe ritual adepts devoted to youтАФas Hotar at the rites, o Agni,
when seeking the gods they provide pleasurable offerings for youтАФthe men with their oblations, with their twisted ritual grass.

Griffith

Here, Api, the arrangers, those attached to thee, elect thee as their Priest in sacred gatherings,
When men with strewn clipt grass and sacrificial gifts offer thee entertainment, piously inclined.

Geldner

Nur dich erw├дhlen da deine Anh├дnger zum Hotri, o Agni, die Meister in den Weisheitsreden, wann die Gottergebenen dir Opfergen├╝sse bereiten, Spenden bringend die Menschen, die das Barhis herumgelegt haben.

Grassmann

Die Ordner, Agni, die dich lieben, w├дhlen dich zu ihrem Priester bei den Opferfesten hier; Wenn dir, versehn mit Tr├дnken und geweihter Streu die frommen M├дnner Opferspeisen setzen vor.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬYours, Agni, is the function of the Hot─Б, yours the duly-performed function of the Pot─Б, yours thefunction of the Neс╣гс╣н─Б, you are the Agni of the sacrificer, yours is the office of the Pra┼Ы─Бst─Б, you act asAdhvaryu, and you are the Brahm─Б and the lord of the mansion in our abode.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

You are the Agni: you are thefire-kindler, or agn─лdhra

Jamison Brereton

Yours, Agni, is the office of Hotar; yours that of Potar in its turn; yours that of Neс╣гс╣нar; you are the Agnidh [=fire-kindler] of the one who
follows truth.
Yours is the office of Pra┼Ы─Бstar; you act as Adhvaryu; you are both the Brahman-priest and the Houselord in our home.

Griffith

Thine is the Herald’s task and Cleanser’s duly timed; Leader art thou, and Kindler for the pious man.
Thou art Director, thou the ministering Priest: thou art the Brahman, Lord and Master in our home.

Geldner

Dir, Agni, kommt das Amt des Hotri zu, dir das Amt des Potri zur rechten Zeit, dir das Amt des Nestri. Du bist der Feueranz├╝nder des, der den rechten Brauch, das Opfer, vollzieht. Dir kommt das Amt des Prasastri zu, du wirkst als Adhvaryu, du bist sowohl der Brahman wie der Herr in unserem Hause.

Grassmann

Dein ist des Priesters, Agni, dein des L├дuterers rechtm├дssig Amt, des F├╝hrers, dein des Ordnenden, Du bist des Frommen Glutentz├╝nder, opferst gern, und Beter bist du, Hausherr du in unserm Haus.

рд╕рд╛рдпрдг-рднрд╛рд╖реНрдпрдореН

рд╣реЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдиреЗ рдЕрдореГрддрд╛рдп рдорд░рдгрдзрд░реНрдорд░рд╣рд┐рддрд╛рдп рддреБрднреНрдпрдВ рдпрдГ рдорд░реНрддреНрдпрдГ рдордиреБрд╖реНрдпрдГ рд╕рдорд┐рдзрд╛ рд╕рдорд┐рдзрдореН ред рджреНрд╡рд┐рддреАрдпрд╛рдпрд╛рдГ тАШрд╕реБрдкрд╛рдВ рд╕реБрд▓реБрдХреН’ рдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рдХрд╛рд░рдГ ред рджрд╛рд╢рддреН рджрджрд╛рддрд┐ рдкреНрд░рдпрдЪреНрдЫрддрд┐ рдЙрдд рд╡рд╛ рдЕрдкрд┐ рд╡рд╛ рд╣рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдХреГрддрд┐ ред рд╣рд╡рд┐рд╖рд╛рдВ рдХреГрддреН рдХрд░рдгрдВ рдпрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рд╕ рд╣рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдХреГрддреН ред рддрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреНрдпрдЬреНрдЮреЗ рд╣рд╡реАрдВрд╖рд┐ рджрджрд╛рддреАрддрд┐ рд╢реЗрд╖рдГ ред рддрд╕реНрдп рдордиреБрд╖реНрдпрд╕реНрдп рд╣реЛрддрд╛ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдирд╛рдорд╛рд╣реНрд╡рд╛рддрд╛ рднрд╡рд╕рд┐ ред рдХрд┐рдВрдЪ рддреНрд╡рдВ рджреВрддреНрдпрдВ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдиреН рдкреНрд░рддрд┐ рджреВрддрдХрд░реНрдо рдХрд░реНрддреБрдВ рдпрд╛рд╕рд┐ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрд╕рд┐ ред рдХрд┐рдВрдЪ рддреНрд╡рдВ рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдорд╛ рднреВрддреНрд╡рд╛рд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рдХрд░реНрдордгрд┐ рдпреБрд╖реНрдорднреНрдпрдорд┐рдорд╛рдирд┐ рд╣рд╡реАрдВрд╖рд┐ рдпрдЬрдорд╛рдиреЗрди рдкреНрд░рд╣рд┐рддрд╛рдиреАрддрд┐ рдЙрдк рдмреНрд░реВрд╖реЗ рдЙрдкрдХреНрд░рдореНрдп рдмреНрд░рд╡реАрд╖рд┐ ред рдХрд┐рдВ рдЪ рддреНрд╡рдВ рдпрдЬрд╕рд┐ рдпрдЬрдорд╛рдиреЛ рднреВрддреНрд╡рд╛ рджреЗрд╡реЗрднреНрдпреЛ рд╣рд╡реАрдВрд╖рд┐ рджрджрд╛рд╕рд┐ ред рдХрд┐рдВрдЪ рддреНрд╡рдВ рддрдерд╛ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡реЛрдХреНрддрдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░реЗрдг рдЕрдзреНрд╡рд░реАрдпрд╕рд┐ рдЕрдзреНрд╡рд░реНрдпреБрд░рд┐рд╡рд╛рдЪрд░рд╕рд┐ ред рдЕрдерд╡рд╛рдиреНрдпрдВ рдпрдЬреНрдЮ рдХрд░реНрддреБрдорд┐рдЪреНрдЫрд╕рд┐ рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThe mortal, Agni, who presents to you, the immortal, fuel at the offering of the oblation– you are hisHot─Б, you go on his errant (to the gods), you direct (the ceremonial), you offer the sacrifice, you act as theofficiating priest.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

You direct: i.e., Agni is the Br─Бhman, the Yajam─Бna and the Adhvaryu

Jamison Brereton

The mortal who for you, the immortal, o Agni, will perform pious work with the kindling stick or by the preparation of the oblation,
for him you become the Hotar; his mission do you undertake. You
speak on his behalf; you perform sacrifice, you act as Adhvaryu
for him.

Griffith

When mortal man presents to thee Immortal God, Agni, his fuel or his sacrificial gift,
Then thou art his Adhvaryu, Hotar, messenger, callest the Gods and orderest the sacrifice.

Geldner

Welcher Sterbliche dir dem Unsterblichen, Agni, mit Brennholz aufwartet oder mit Opferwerk, dessen Hotri wirst du; f├╝r ihn tust du Botendienst, sprichst den G├╢ttern zu, opferst, besorgst die heilige Handlung.

Grassmann

Dem Sterblichen, der, Agni, dir Unsterblichem mit Brennholz huldigt oder auch mit Opfertrank, Dem bist du Opfrer, gehst f├╝r ihn auf Botschaft aus, du sprichst f├╝r ihn, du opferst, thust des Priesters Dienst.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay these laudatory words, these eulogistic verses, these voices (proceeding) from us, reach him thegiver of wealth, J─Бtavedas; these wealth- desiring (words) in which when they are perfected, the perfecterdelights.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

These hereтАФthe thoughts, speeches, verses, songs, and good praises from usтАФhave come together for him,
for J─Бtavedas the good oneтАФgoods-seeking (praises) in which he will take pleasure as their strengthener, though they are (already) strong.

Griffith

From us these hymns in concert have gone forth to him, these. holy words, these Rcas, songs and eulogies,
Eager for wealth, to Jatavedas fain for wealth: when they have waxen strong they please their Strengthener.

Geldner

Diese Dichtungen, Reden, Verse, Lobesworte, Preislieder sind von uns aus vereint zu ihm gekommen, nach Gut verlangend, zu dem guten Jatavedas, an denen er seine Freude haben soll, sie noch h├╢her machend, obwohl sie schon hoch sind.

Grassmann

Ihm sind von uns her diese Lieder zugeeilt, Gebete, Spr├╝che, Hymnen voll des sch├╢nsten Lobs Dem Wesenkenner, von dem guten heischend Gut, die kr├дftigen, an denen sich der Kr├дft’ger labt.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬI will address this new laudatory hymn to the ancient Agni, who is gratified (by praise). May he hear uс╣гMay I be in the centre of his heart, to touch it, like a loving well-attired wife (in the heart) of her husband.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

I would proclaim this good praise here, a newer one, to him, the age-old, who is eager for it: let him hear us.
May it come very close, to touch his heart, like an eager wife, richly
dressed, to her husband.

Griffith

This newest eulogy will I speak forth to him, the Ancient One who loves it. May he hear our voice.
May it come near his heart and make it stir with love, as a fond well-dressed matron clings about her lord.

Geldner

Dieses neueste Loblied will ich dem Uralten aufsagen, ihm, der darnach verlangt; er h├╢re auf uns! Es m├╢ge ihm nahe zu Herzen gehen, um es zu r├╝hren, wie die verliebte sch├╢ngekleidete Frau des Gatten.

Grassmann

Dem alten will ich singen dieses neuste Lob, ihm, der es gern hat, m├╢ge er erh├╢ren uns; Es m├╢ge recht vertraut ber├╝hren nun sein Herz, so wie die schmucke Gattin liebend den Gemahl.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬI offer graceful praise with all my heart to Agni, the drinker of water, whose back is sprinkled withSoma, the ordainer (of the rite), to whom vigorous horses and bulls and barren cows and sheep are consignedas burnt offerings.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

I offer: Yajus. 20.78 has janaya, offer, perhaps addressed to the Adhvaryu

Jamison Brereton

(For him) into whom horses, bulls, oxen, mated cows, rams, once released, are poured out [=offered],
for the k─лl─Бla-drinker who has soma on his back, for the ritual adept
I generate with my heart a pleasing thoughtтАФfor Agni.

Griffith

He in whom horses, bulls, oxen, and barren cows, and rams, when duly set apart, are offered up,-
To Agni, Soma-sprinkled, drinker of sweet juice, Disposer, with my heart I bring a fair hymn forth.

Geldner

In welchem Rosse, Stiere, Ochsen, g├╝ste K├╝he, Widder zum Opfer freigelassen geopfert werden, auf den S├╝├Яtranktrinker mit Soma auf dem R├╝cken, auf den Meister mache ich mit dem Herzen ein Gedicht, das dem Agni genehm ist.

Grassmann

Zu welchem Rosse, Stiere, Ochsen, K├╝he auch und Widder man entsendet und als Opfer bringt, Dem Agni, welcher S├╝sses trinkt und Soma tr├дgt, dem Ordner zeug’ ich aus dem Herzen sch├╢nes Lied.

English translation:

тАЬThe oblation has been poured, Agni, into your mouth, like butter into the ladle, like Soma into thespoon. Bestow upon us riches conferring food, (comprehending) male progeny, excellent renowned andabundant.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

An oblation has been poured into your mouth, Agni, like ghee into a ladle, like soma into a cup.
Place in us prize-gaining wealth, rich in heroes, celebrated,
glorious, lofty.

Griffith

Into thy mouth is poured the offering, Agni, as Soma into cup, oil into ladle.
Vouchsafe us wealth. strength-winning, blest with heroes, wealth lofty, praised by men, and full of splendour.
